a bhrātur ādeśam ādāya lakṣmaṇo vā paraṃtapaḥ
c sa kimarthaṃ naravaro na māṃ rakṣati rāghavaḥ
a śaktau tau puruṣavyāghrau vāyvagnisamatejasau
c surāṇām api durdharṣau kimarthaṃ mām upekṣataḥ
a mamaiva duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃ cin mahad asti na saṃśayaḥ
c samarthau sahitau yan māṃ nāpekṣete paraṃtapau
a vaidehyā vacanaṃ śrutvā karuṇaṃ sāśrubhāṣitam
c punar apy aham āryāṃ tām idaṃ vacanam abruvam
a tvacchokavimukho rāmo devi satyena te śape
c rāme duḥkhābhibhūte ca lakṣmaṇaḥ paritapyate
a kathaṃ cid bhavatī dṛṣṭā na kālaḥ pariśocitum
c imaṃ muhūrtaṃ duḥkhānām antaṃ drakṣyasi bhāmini
a tāv ubhau naraśārdūlau rājaputrāv ariṃdamau
c tvaddarśanakṛtotsāhau laṅkāṃ bhasmīkariṣyataḥ
a hatvā ca samare raudraṃ rāvaṇaṃ saha bāndhavam
c rāghavas tvāṃ mahābāhuḥ svāṃ purīṃ nayate dhruvam
a yat tu rāmo vijānīyād abhijñānam anindite
c prītisaṃjananaṃ tasya pradātuṃ tattvam arhasi
a sābhivīkṣya diśaḥ sarvā veṇyudgrathanam uttamam
c muktvā vastrād dadau mahyaṃ maṇim etaṃ mahābala
a pratigṛhya maṇiṃ divyaṃ tava heto raghūttama
c śirasā saṃpraṇamyainām aham āgamane tvare
a gamane ca kṛtotsāham avekṣya varavarṇinī
c vivardhamānaṃ ca hi mām uvāca janakātmajā
e aśrupūrṇamukhī dīnā bāṣpasaṃdigdhabhāṣiṇī
a hanuman siṃhasaṃkāśau tāv ubhau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c sugrīvaṃ ca sahāmātyaṃ sarvān brūyā anāmayam
a yathā ca sa mahābāhur māṃ tārayati rāghavaḥ
c asmād duḥkhāmbusaṃrodhāt tat samādhātum arhasi
a imaṃ ca tīvraṃ mama śokavegaṃ
rakṣobhir ebhiḥ paribhartsanaṃ ca
c brūyās tu rāmasya gataḥ samīpaṃ
śivaś ca te 'dhvāstu haripravīra
a etat tavāryā nṛparājasiṃha
sītā vacaḥ prāha viṣādapūrvam
c etac ca buddhvā gaditaṃ mayā tvaṃ
śraddhatsva sītāṃ kuśalāṃ samagrām
a athāham uttaraṃ devyā punar uktaḥ sasaṃbhramam
c tava snehān naravyāghra sauhāryād anumānya ca
a evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ vācyo rāmo dāśarathis tvayā
c yathā mām āpnuyāc chīghraṃ hatvā rāvaṇam āhave
a yadi vā manyase vīra vasaikāham ariṃdama
c kasmiṃś cit saṃvṛte deśe viśrāntaḥ śvo gamiṣyasi
a mama cāpy alpabhāgyāyāḥ sāmnidhyāt tava vānara
c asya śokavipākasya muhūrtaṃ syād vimokṣaṇam
a gate hi tvayi vikrānte punarāgamanāya vai
c prāṇānām api saṃdeho mama syān nātra saṃśayaḥ
a tavādarśanajaḥ śoko bhūyo māṃ paritāpayet
c duḥkhād duḥkhaparābhūtāṃ durgatāṃ duḥkhabhāginīm
a ayaṃ tu vīrasaṃdehas tiṣṭhatīva mamāgrataḥ
c sumahāṃs tvatsahāyeṣu haryṛkṣeṣu asaṃśayaḥ
a kathaṃ nu khalu duṣpāraṃ tariṣyanti mahodadhim
c tāni haryṛkṣasainyāni tau vā naravarātmajau
a trayāṇām eva bhūtānāṃ sāgarasyāsya laṅghane
c śaktiḥ syād vainateyasya vāyor vā tava vānagha
a tad asmin kāryaniyoge vīraivaṃ duratikrame
c kiṃ paśyasi samādhānaṃ brūhi kāryavidāṃ vara
a kāmam asya tvam evaikaḥ kāryasya parisādhane
c paryāptaḥ paravīraghna yaśasyas te balodayaḥ
a balaiḥ samagrair yadi māṃ hatvā rāvaṇam āhave
c vijayī svāṃ purīṃ rāmo nayet tat syād yaśaskaram
a yathāhaṃ tasya vīrasya vanād upadhinā hṛtā
c rakṣasā tad bhayād eva tathā nārhati rāghavaḥ
a balais tu saṃkulāṃ kṛtvā laṅkāṃ parabalārdanaḥ
c māṃ nayed yadi kākutsthas tat tasya sadṛśaṃ bhavet
a tad yathā tasya vikrāntam anurūpaṃ mahātmanaḥ
c bhavaty āhavaśūrasya tathā tvam upapādaya
a tad arthopahitaṃ vākyaṃ praśritaṃ hetusaṃhitam
c niśamyāhaṃ tataḥ śeṣaṃ vākyam uttaram abruvam
a devi haryṛkṣasainyānām īśvaraḥ plavatāṃ varaḥ
c sugrīvaḥ sattvasaṃpannas tavārthe kṛtaniścayaḥ
a tasya vikramasaṃpannāḥ sattvavanto mahābalāḥ
c manaḥsaṃkalpasaṃpātā nideśe harayaḥ sthitāḥ
a yeṣāṃ nopari nādhastān na tiryak sajjate gatiḥ
c na ca karmasu sīdanti mahatsv amitatejasaḥ
a asakṛt tair mahābhāgair vānarair balasaṃyutaiḥ
c pradakṣiṇīkṛtā bhūmir vāyumārgānusāribhiḥ
a madviśiṣṭāś ca tulyāś ca santi tatra vanaukasaḥ
c mattaḥ pratyavaraḥ kaś cin nāsti sugrīvasaṃnidhau
a ahaṃ tāvad iha prāptaḥ kiṃ punas te mahābalāḥ
c na hi prakṛṣṭāḥ preṣyante preṣyante hītare janāḥ
a tad alaṃ paritāpena devi manyur vyapaitu te
c ekotpātena te laṅkām eṣyanti hariyūthapāḥ
a mama pṛṣṭhagatau tau ca candrasūryāv ivoditau
c tvatsakāśaṃ mahābhāge nṛsiṃhāv āgamiṣyataḥ
a arighnaṃ siṃhasaṃkāśaṃ kṣipraṃ drakṣyasi rāghavam
c lakṣmaṇaṃ ca dhanuṣpāṇiṃ laṅkā dvāram upasthitam
a nakhadaṃṣṭrāyudhān vīrān siṃhaśārdūlavikramān
c vānarān vānarendrābhān kṣipraṃ drakṣyasi saṃgatān
a śailāmbudan nikāśānāṃ laṅkāmalayasānuṣu
c nardatāṃ kapimukhyānām acirāc choṣyase svanam
a nivṛttavanavāsaṃ ca tvayā sārdham ariṃdamam
c abhiṣiktam ayodhyāyāṃ kṣipraṃ drakṣyasi rāghavam
a tato mayā vāgbhir adīnabhāṣiṇī
śivābhir iṣṭābhir abhiprasāditā
c jagāma śāntiṃ mama maithilātmajā
tavāpi śokena tathābhipīḍitā
